\DoxyCodeLine{1846   \textcolor{comment}{// When should\_track\_json\_source is true, we use val\_node to record current}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1847   \textcolor{comment}{// JSON value's parse node.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1848   \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1849   \textcolor{comment}{// For primitive values, the val\_node is the source string of the JSON value.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1850   \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1851   \textcolor{comment}{// For JSObject values, the val\_node is an ObjectHashTable in which the key is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1852   \textcolor{comment}{// the property name and the first value is the property value's parse}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1853   \textcolor{comment}{// node. The order in which properties are defined may be different from the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1854   \textcolor{comment}{// order in which properties are enumerated when calling}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1855   \textcolor{comment}{// InternalizeJSONProperty for the JSObject value. E.g., the JSON source}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1856   \textcolor{comment}{// string is '\{"{}a"{}: 1, "{}1"{}: 2\}', and the properties enumerate order is ["{}1"{},}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1857   \textcolor{comment}{// "{}a"{}]. Moreover, properties may be defined repeatedly in the JSON string.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1858   \textcolor{comment}{// E.g., the JSON string is '\{"{}a"{}: 1, "{}a"{}: 1\}', and the properties enumerate}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1859   \textcolor{comment}{// order is ["{}a"{}]. So we cannot use the FixedArray to record the properties's}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1860   \textcolor{comment}{// parse node by the order in which properties are defined and we use a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1861   \textcolor{comment}{// ObjectHashTable here to record the property name and the property's parse}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1862   \textcolor{comment}{// node. We then look up the property's parse node by the property name when}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1863   \textcolor{comment}{// calling InternalizeJSONProperty. The second value associated with the key}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1864   \textcolor{comment}{// is the property value's snapshot.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1865   \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1866   \textcolor{comment}{// For JSArray values, the val\_node is a FixedArray containing the parse nodes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1867   \textcolor{comment}{// and snapshots of the elements.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1868   \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1869   \textcolor{comment}{// For information about snapshotting, see below.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1870   Handle<Object> val\_node;}
